  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_0dc25398-7872-4e58-a701-d925fab363bf'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();

<span id="freeTextContainer11489731324958842460"><b>
  <i>From the <i>USA Today</i> Best Selling <i>Sweet Home</i> Series, comes <i>Sweet Fall</i>; a tale of heartache, beating the odds and finding strength in the most unlikeliest of places.</i>
</b><br/><br/><i>We all have secrets.<br/><br/>Secrets well buried.<br/><br/>Until we find the one soul who makes the burden of such secrets just that little bit easier to bear.</i><br/><br/>Lexington "Lexi" Hart is a senior at the University of Alabama. Surro</span>
  <span id="freeText11489731324958842460" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>From the <i>USA Today</i> Best Selling <i>Sweet Home</i> Series, comes <i>Sweet Fall</i>; a tale of heartache, beating the odds and finding strength in the most unlikeliest of places.</i>
</b><br /><br /><i>We all have secrets.<br /><br />Secrets well buried.<br /><br />Until we find the one soul who makes the burden of such secrets just that little bit easier to bear.</i><br /><br />Lexington "Lexi" Hart is a senior at the University of Alabama. Surrounded by her best friends, her loving family and having fulfilled her life-long dream of making the Crimson Tide cheer squad, everything is going exactly as she always dreamed it would. But beneath her happy exterior, demons lurk, threatening to jeopardize everything Lexi has worked to achieve. When events in her life become too much to cope with, Lexi finds herself spiraling down into the realm of her biggest fear. Lexi falls hard, victim once again to the only thing that can destroy her and, on the way, finds herself falling straight into the dangerous tattooed arms of a guy from the wrong side of the tracks.<br /><br />Austin Carillo, starting Wide Receiver for the Alabama Crimson Tide, must get picked in this year's NFL draft. He needs it. His brothers need it. Most importantly, his mother desperately needs it. Brought up in a world where the poor are forgotten, the sick are left to fend for themselves and no hero miraculously appears to pull you out of hell, Austin had no other choice but to make a living on the wrong side of the law—until football offered Austin the break to get his life back on track. But when a family tragedy drags him back into the clutches of the gang he believed he had left far behind, Austin finds himself falling. Falling back into criminal ways and falling deep into a suffocating darkness. Until a troubled yet kindred spirit stumbles across his path, where Austin quickly finds he is falling for a young woman, a young woman who might just have the power to save him from his worst enemy: himself.<br /><br />Can two troubled souls find a lasting peace together? Or will they finally succumb to the demons threatening to destroy them?<br /><br />New Adult/Contemporary Romance novel—contains adult content, sexual situations and mature topics. Suited for ages 18 and up.<br /><br />Can be read as a stand-alone novel.</span>

<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">Release day: Augst 26th<br/><br/>Previous books are: Sweet Home and Sweet Fall - Sweet Home is about Molly and Rome; Sweet Home is Molly's pov and Sweet Rome is<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">Release day: Augst 26th<br /><br />Previous books are: Sweet Home and Sweet Fall - Sweet Home is about Molly and Rome; Sweet Home is Molly's pov and Sweet Rome is Rome's pov. Austin is in these books a little but in theory you don't have to read them to be able to read Sweet Fall. However, there are some spoilers about the previous books in there in case you wanted to read them.<br /><br />Sanne - Scandalous Book Blog<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1010778396" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1010778396?book_show_action=true">Jul 29, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11284813-christy?shelf=2017-audio">2017-audio</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1010778396" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11389904839406846267"><b>5+ devastating stars!!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/03fbe4b2-6e57-432a-bbf9-ce8021593b78_zpse41dfd8d.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409922352i/11040150.jpg' alt=' photo 03fbe4b2-6e57-432a-bbf9-ce8021593b78_zpse41dfd8d.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Do you ever read a book thats so beautiful, yet so tragic and painful when your done you just don’t know what to do with yourself? Your heart is happy- but it still hurts so much. So you just sit and think about the book, cry some more and try to move on with a new read… that was my <i>Sweet Fall</i> experience. I did not expect this book to hit me so hard. I didn’t just cry a few tears, it was a river.<br/><br/>I loved the first two books in Tillie Cole’s <i>Sweet Home</i> series, but she re</span>
  <span id="freeText11389904839406846267" style="display:none"><b>5+ devastating stars!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/03fbe4b2-6e57-432a-bbf9-ce8021593b78_zpse41dfd8d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409922352i/11040150.jpg" alt=" photo 03fbe4b2-6e57-432a-bbf9-ce8021593b78_zpse41dfd8d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Do you ever read a book thats so beautiful, yet so tragic and painful when your done you just don’t know what to do with yourself? Your heart is happy- but it still hurts so much. So you just sit and think about the book, cry some more and try to move on with a new read… that was my <i>Sweet Fall</i> experience. I did not expect this book to hit me so hard. I didn’t just cry a few tears, it was a river.<br><br>I loved the first two books in Tillie Cole’s <i>Sweet Home</i> series, but she really surprised me with this book. It was so different than the first two, and it was by far my favorite of the three. Austin and Lexi’s story had a profound effect on me. It’s a story I won’t soon forget.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/7e96cabd-649b-49ea-b950-ddd5503c04ed_zpsa22b27de.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409922352i/11040151.jpg" alt=" photo 7e96cabd-649b-49ea-b950-ddd5503c04ed_zpsa22b27de.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Lexi is a girl with some serious issues. Those who know anyone with an eating disorder, know it’s like addiction. You are never completely healed. You’re just in some sort of remission. Lexi has been okay the last 3 years of college. Her new friends know noting about her past. Her black hair and ‘war paint’ is the mask she wears. She hides anything bad- always cheerful and happy. But her disorder is back with a vengeance. <br><br>Then there is Austin. Austin has a wonderful (yet very sick) mother, but had a rough upbringing. Being introduced to the gang world early in life, he’s made his way out. He’s the wide receiver for the Tide and he’s on the fast track to the NFL. When his mother’s condition worsens, Austin is forced to make some tough choices. Choices for him and his brothers. Things he thought he would never do again. Family is all Austin has. He has to do what he has to do for them. But he meets a broken girl named Lexi. And it changes everything.<br> <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/ac064bc1-b784-4eba-94f8-06656ca483bf_zps7e6b094f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409922352i/11040152.jpg" alt=" photo ac064bc1-b784-4eba-94f8-06656ca483bf_zps7e6b094f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Austin and Lexi make the most unlikely pair. At first, their relationship is very strained. Lexi see’s something she shouldn’t have, and Austin isn’t happy about it. They try to keep their distance, but they are drawn together. They both are a mess. They both have secrets. But they both understand each other. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“We all have secrets, Austin. Some people’s are just bigger than others, that’s all.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> <br>Both are living such different lives than what is perceived. Both have issues- have scars. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote> “So you see, Pix, I have scars too. It’ just mine are on the outside where everyone can see.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Everything is a mess in both of their lives. The only solace they find is in each other. They both have found that one person who see’s their demons, their scars and accepts them. The one person they can talk to freely. Neither one can go to their friends about these issues. But they have each other.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/8f21c653-0b4f-4e0e-a011-c539ff8dfe5e_zpsc3f28b22.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409922352i/11040153.jpg" alt=" photo 8f21c653-0b4f-4e0e-a011-c539ff8dfe5e_zpsc3f28b22.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Until something bigger happens, then they don’t. <br><i>
  <blockquote>
    <b> I’m lost without you. I can’t breathe without you. Without you here, all I can do is fall.</b>
  </blockquote>
</i><br><br>Both characters in this story were completely broken and flawed, yet somehow they were able to be strong for the other person. Austin looks so dangerous with his tattoo’s and his tough exterior, but the way he cares about Lexi and treats her is inspiring. His mom and the way he was with his brothers- I just fell in love with him even more. He may not have always made the right choices, but what he did, he did out of loyalty and love. <br><br>Lexi’s story broke me. Her inner thoughts and the voice- I just couldn’t handle it at times. It was so hard to read. I admire her strength. I can’t imagine dealing with something like that inside myself. It was beyond difficult to get through some scenes. The tears just kept dripping down my face. My god I was so happy she had Austin. I love that he saw the real beauty in her. <br><br>I’m glad this story was in dual pov. I feel like we got so much out of it by being able to be in both Lexi and Austin’s head. This book really effected me- it moved me, it broke my heart and it pieced me back together. I know Ally’s story is next in the <i>Sweet Home</i> series, but I have the highest of hopes that Tillie will write us a Levi book. I adored that kid and would love to read a story about him! <br><br>Overall- this was one of the best books I’ve read this year. If your looking for a heartbreakingly beautiful book with damaged characters, fantastic writing and one that will change your outlook on a lot of things, pick this up! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/2c17a64d-298d-4313-bc3a-837dd425a6d1_zpsb12a601a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409922352i/11040154.jpg" alt=" photo 2c17a64d-298d-4313-bc3a-837dd425a6d1_zpsb12a601a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> “Pix… you’re so fuckin’ beautiful. You, like this… perfection.”<br> “I’m beautiful with you.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="11389904839406846267" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_759646596" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/759646596" />
    <a title="Patrycja" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6852653-patrycja"><img alt="Patrycja" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1586460589p2/6852653.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/759646596?book_show_action=true">Nov 08, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patrycja" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patrycja" href="/user/show/6852653-patrycja">Patrycja</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=must-read">must-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=2014">2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=arc-s">arc-s</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer759646596" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7843194225493139152"><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420433._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Title:</b> Sweet Fall<br/><b>Series:</b> Sweet Home #3<br/><b>Author:</b> Tillie Cole <br/><b>Release Date: </b> 26 August, 2014<br/><b>Rating:</b> 4.5 stars<br/><b>Cliffhanger:</b>. No<br/><b> HEA: </b> <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ Yes  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420434._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408283897i/10831564.jpg' width='400' height='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>Sweet Fall </i>is powerful experience; it’s gritty and raw and so true. It’s incredibly painful read, full of angst, sorrow and agonizing loneliness. Reading it is bitter sweet. The story behind our two main characters will make your heart clench and hurt; the angst, the pain, all the emotions that Tillie Cole’s perfectly captured will ma</span>
  <span id="freeText7843194225493139152" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420433._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Title:</b> Sweet Fall<br><b>Series:</b> Sweet Home #3<br><b>Author:</b> Tillie Cole <br><b>Release Date: </b> 26 August, 2014<br><b>Rating:</b> 4.5 stars<br><b>Cliffhanger:</b>. No<br><b> HEA: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420434._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408283897i/10831564.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Sweet Fall </i>is powerful experience; it’s gritty and raw and so true. It’s incredibly painful read, full of angst, sorrow and agonizing loneliness. Reading it is bitter sweet. The story behind our two main characters will make your heart clench and hurt; the angst, the pain, all the emotions that Tillie Cole’s perfectly captured will make you hangover for weeks. <br><br><i>
  <b>"We were both just too messed up to ever be with each other in the way we needed to be. Two shooting stars that burned out too quickly, never quite reaching each other's skies."</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408283897i/10831566.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Lexi</b> is faking everything in her life. Her happiness, her good health, being strong. Behind the dark make up and black dyed hair, she’s scared, fragile and broken. With her friends she chooses to wear a mask of the happy girl she was once, but when she’s alone… she’s ugly and sad. She’s suffering from disorder that slowly eats her alive. And although she's dealing with her anorexia with the help of her parents and doctor, no one else knows how she sees herself in the mirror. <br><br>After few years of not cheering, she decides it’s finally time to go back to doing something she loves so much. Even if it means, she has to deal with people looking at her… ‘fat’ body.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408283897i/10831568.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Austin</b> is a wide receiver for Crimson Tide’s football team. He’s doing everything he can to make it to NFL and help his family. Thanks to Rome and his brother - Axel, he had opportunity to leave Heighters, the gang he was in. But now that his mother is even worse than before, and his brothers are dealing coke on his campus, he’s really damn close to being expelled… <br><br>That’s when he meets Lexi, dark little pixie in not the best circumstances, things seem to get even more complicated.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408283897i/10831570.jpg" width="400" height="550" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>"I have fallen in love with you. The broken boy who has only ever known trouble and strife. Yet the broken boy who managed to put this broken girl back together, at least for a while."</b>
</i><br><br><i>Sweet Fall</i> is written in dual point of view, and thank god for that! Seeing both Lexi and Austin completely bare before me, with all their heartbreaking secrets was something that really moved me. The effect wouldn’t be the same if that was not the case. Being able to sneak a peek into their souls… hurt. I won’t be sugar-coating; what both of them had to live through is not a walk in the park. It’s horrible and gut-wrenching. And every reader needs to be ready for lots of emotional moments and very high level of angst. The fluffy kind of love we got in Sweet Home doesn’t exist in Lexi and Austin’s novel. They are too broken, too scared to have an easy relationship. <br><br>There were moments when I felt mentally overwhelmed; especially when Lexi’s issues started showing its ugly head. I’ve been very uncomfortable then. Seeing her starving herself was just too much sometimes. I felt like someone was cutting my heart into pieces. I was mad at her for acting so stupid, though I knew that she was doing her best. She was a fighter and I admired her for that, but sometimes… ugh, I just felt so overcame with it. <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408283897i/10831573.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Austin was great, strong character who also made quite some mistakes along the way. I adored him, I really did, but I also found him rough around the edges and standoffish. Which I guess made him more appealing, as he was very real, not-so-perfect hero. There were situations when my heart was bleeding for him, so so much. I was on the verge of tears more times I could count. <br><br>Sweet Fall is nothing like the previous book in this series, we all fell in love with, Austin and Lexi will quickly make you forget about Rome and Molly. Their story is just too laud, too captivating to be able to think about something else. It’s dark and real and it hurts to read it, but it’s worth it! <br><br><br><b>ARC kindly provided by the author, Tillie Cole, in exchange for an honest review</b><br><br><b>FOLLOW SMOKIN HOT BOOK BLOG ON: <b><br><br><a href="https://twitter.com/BlogSmokin/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img alt="Twitter" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391768351i/8452934.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="http://facebook.com/smokinhotbookblog" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img alt="Facebook" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391768485i/8452963.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="https://plus.google.com/113975606544004548659" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img alt="Google Plus" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391768485i/8452964.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="http://smokinhotbookblog.blogspot.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img alt="Smokin Hot Book Blog" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391769122i/8453144.png" width="32" height="32" <div id="review_1145309649" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1145309649" />
    <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei"><img alt="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421992465p2/2551178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1145309649?book_show_action=true">Dec 28, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei">Lady Vigilante (Feifei)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=contemporary-duckie">contemporary-duckie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=i-trust-my-friends">i-trust-my-friends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=new-adult-express">new-adult-express</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=bad-boys">bad-boys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=sweet-hero">sweet-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=dark-reads">dark-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=depressed">depressed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=cry-me-a-river">cry-me-a-river</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1145309649" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1129904744252989376"><b>4.5 stars!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419924091i/13147629._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Goodreads really needs half stars because this book was more than a 4 but not quite a 5 star read. Nevertheless, this book made me lose my marbles and break down and ugly cry…definitely one of the more heavy and dark NA romances I’ve read this year. Whatever expectations I had, I didn’t count on this book being so gutwrenchingly emotional. The characters were yanking at my heartstrings right from the beginning, and little by little, the emotion built up until it exploded in the last 2</span>
  <span id="freeText1129904744252989376" style="display:none"><b>4.5 stars!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419924091i/13147629._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Goodreads really needs half stars because this book was more than a 4 but not quite a 5 star read. Nevertheless, this book made me lose my marbles and break down and ugly cry…definitely one of the more heavy and dark NA romances I’ve read this year. Whatever expectations I had, I didn’t count on this book being so gutwrenchingly emotional. The characters were yanking at my heartstrings right from the beginning, and little by little, the emotion built up until it exploded in the last 20% of the book and basically nuked my heart. Thanks Tillie Cole. <br><br>But I’m getting ahead of myself again. Back to the beginning…<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419924091i/13147630._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>On the outside, Lexi Hart is a perfect college student who seems to have it all: loving family, supportive friends, and a spot on the cheer squad. But underneath, every day is a struggle for her and she’s barely keeping up. Unknown to most, Lexi is anorexic. Her body image worries and thoughts hurt her deeper than any blade could and ashamed of herself, she concocts a mask to hide behind when she’s with friends. Only alone, can she be her true self. Only alone, can she be free to give into her anorexic temptations. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419924091i/13147631._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Austin Carillo has a boatload of problems, all invisible to most. Coming from a poor and unstable home life with a sick mother and two brothers to look after, Austin sees football as his only way out of his shithole life. But it isn’t enough and with gang problems giving him trouble, Austin is cornered between pursuing his football dream and living like a lowlife like he’s perceived to be, all in the name of providing for his family. <br><br>Austin and Lexi’s romance seemed improbable at the beginning because they were so different. Aside from their circle of friends knowing each other, there is literally no overlap that should’ve happened between them so the fact that their romance did happen was totally unexpected and made it all the more intriguing. Perhaps it was because they were both broken and felt like they were shouldering the world that they had this deep, intense connection, but whatever the reason they’re able to let down their guard and be open with each other.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419924091i/13147632._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Reading about these characters individually and what they had to go through with all the problems in their lives gave my heart a big squeeze, but that was nothing compared to the scenes where they were a couple. <br><br><i>
  <b>“Why the war paint, Pix?”<br>“Why the tattoos?”</b>
</i><br><br>I’m not even going to sugarcoat it – I felt overwhelmed. Reading about Lexi’s anorexia hurt, like in my chest kinda hurt, and it was all portrayed in such a raw and gritty manner I couldn’t help but be moved. Reading about Austin’s poor home life, his very real and heartbreaking struggle to keep his family together while trying so hard to make his football dream come true…all of that combined was a lot to process and emotionally digest down. And as mentioned before, all of this culminated and completely exploded in the last 20% of the book, leaving me a sobbing mess.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419924091i/13147633._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But at the same time, I didn’t fully love the romance part. I mean, it was very clear to me that these two characters belonged and complemented each other perfectly, but because there was just SO much going on – Lexi’s illness, Austin’s home life – plus tons of external conflict ranging from gang business to side character drama, I felt like the actual romance wasn’t given enough attention, hence I had to deduct half a star. <br><br>Regardless, this is a book that is guaranteed to make you FEEL and ultimately, that’s what I was looking for when I decided to read this book so overall, this one’s a winner for me!<br><br><u>Sweet Fall</u> is a NA romance standalone and the 3rd book in the Sweet Home series. It can be read without reading the first two books and the events in this book run parallel to those in the first one, <u>Sweet Home.</u></span>
  <a data-text-id="1129904744252989376" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1030314484" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2382846422817978282"><a href='http://amzn.to/1NLAma0' rel='nofollow noopener'>ONLY .99 currently</a><br/><br/><b>4.5 Heartbreaking Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409663652i/11005757._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Wow! This is story is so much different then the other books in the series. <i>Sweet Fall</i> is such an emotional read, their stories broke my heart. <br/><br/>Lexi Hart is a senior cheerleader for the University of Alabama, and Austin Carillo is the star wide receiver - sounds like the perfect college life, right? This is the perfect story of things not being as they seem. Lexi may be a varsity cheerleader, but that doesn’t change fact that she battles with an eating di</span>
  <span id="freeText2382846422817978282" style="display:none"><a href="http://amzn.to/1NLAma0" rel="nofollow noopener">ONLY .99 currently</a><br><br><b>4.5 Heartbreaking Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409663652i/11005757._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Wow! This is story is so much different then the other books in the series. <i>Sweet Fall</i> is such an emotional read, their stories broke my heart. <br><br>Lexi Hart is a senior cheerleader for the University of Alabama, and Austin Carillo is the star wide receiver - sounds like the perfect college life, right? This is the perfect story of things not being as they seem. Lexi may be a varsity cheerleader, but that doesn’t change fact that she battles with an eating disorder. While Austin is the star on the field he is barely surviving off the field with his family's gang relation and dying mother. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409663652i/11005758._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This story blew me away and broke my heart! I had no idea the internal battle and thoughts of someone with an eating disorder. Now, I will say this Tillie Cole does state that these are not everyone’s thoughts and she isn’t a doctor. Okay, back on track. My point being until you have lived that life you can’t imagine what they go through. I have had friends with eating disorders, watched Lifetime movies, and read about them, but I have never really thought about the constant battle they face. I am so glad Ms. Cole was brave enough to write about this, it definitely makes me more sympathetic and caution of the possible signs. <br><br>The story of Austin’s struggles was just as heart breaking and beautiful. Struggling with knowing what is right, but what you have to do for survival. I loved how Austin was with his mother, brothers and Lexi. <br><br>Since this story is told in dual POV you are able to grasp the challenges and heartbreak both characters feel. <br><br><b>
  <i>If I could go back in time, I would find you. I would search the world to seek you out and make you fall in love with me once more.</i>
</b><br><br>I loved this story, and highly recommend!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409580602i/10994824.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></span>

<div id="review_1135120275" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1135120275" />
    <a title="Catarina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina"><img alt="Catarina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514808293p2/11538033.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1135120275?book_show_action=true">Dec 18, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Catarina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Catarina" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina">Catarina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/22919478-sweet-fall">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=the-bad-boy-look">the-bad-boy-look</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=girls-like-athletes">girls-like-athletes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=cotton-candy-romance">cotton-candy-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=cat-heart-these-books">cat-heart-these-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=oh-the-angst">oh-the-angst</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1135120275" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8764713499454724373"><b>4,5 Pixie Stars. </b><br/>	<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418939852i/12951534.jpg' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Lexi and Austin met in college and they are perfect on the outside. He’s the hot Italian guy who plays on the football team. She is the goth happy girl who is in the cheerleading team. However, on the inside they are broken. Austin comes from a bad place, his mother is very sick and his brothers are connect to drug dealing gang who are dealing in college. Lexi is anorexic and is trying to hide her battle from everyone and pretending to be happy. What happen when two broken worl</span>
  <span id="freeText8764713499454724373" style="display:none"><b>4,5 Pixie Stars. </b><br>	<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418939852i/12951534.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lexi and Austin met in college and they are perfect on the outside. He’s the hot Italian guy who plays on the football team. She is the goth happy girl who is in the cheerleading team. However, on the inside they are broken. Austin comes from a bad place, his mother is very sick and his brothers are connect to drug dealing gang who are dealing in college. Lexi is anorexic and is trying to hide her battle from everyone and pretending to be happy. What happen when two broken worlds meet? They collide. And what begins to be loving and beautiful is soon haunted for their ghosts and their pasts. How can they heal the other, when they can’t even heal themselves? There are battles that are destined to being lost, and it’s up to them to give up or keep fighting. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418939852i/12951535._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Tillie Cole is turning into one of my favorite authors, ever. It’s amazing how she grabs two broken souls and bring them together creating an amazing journey of love and redemption. This book was emotional, raw, beautiful and sometimes downward painful. It messed with my emotions in such way that I know that this one of these books, the ones that will never leave my memory. The only reason I’m not giving it five stars is because if there’s a limit for angst in a book, these book definitely broke it. And the fact that it was a brilliant broken story, doesn’t completely compensate the fact that I finished it wanting to drink an entire bottle of vodka. (I didn’t do it, in case you’re wondering.) <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402872274i/10002999.jpg" width="350" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Rating: </b> 4,5 Stars. <br> <b>Characters Development: </b> How broken and beautiful these two are. I don’t know what he is to suffer from a eating disorder, but it can’t be easy believing that we’re re never good enough, that you’re never going to be beautiful. Tillie Cole did a great work creating Lexi and I loved to see her journey and how she slowly strive away from it. Austin was also an amazing guy and I loved how he acted with Pix even when his own life was a mess. I loved the two of them together, they were beautiful. And I also loved to see more of the others. And seriously… who will be Abby’s love interest in the next book?? Because I have not a single clue!! <br> <b>Steam: </b> Meh. <br> <b>Sensible Subjects: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Drugs and gangs. Death. Eating disorders. Want more? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <b>Love Triangle: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <b>HEA: </b>	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="8764713499454724373" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1047740864?book_show_action=true">Sep 06, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brandi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brandi" href="/user/show/5494655-brandi">Brandi</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5494655-brandi?shelf=2014-favorite">2014-favorite</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1047740864" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17464236991593724153"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410190201i/11072137._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='355' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This book put me through the ringer. It was heartbreaking, painful and it left it's mark. I had to take a few breaks, <i>Sweet Fall</i> is not an easy read.<br/><br/><i>
  <b>We were both just too messed up to ever be with each other in the way we needed to be. Two shooting stars that burned out too quickly, never quite reaching each other's skies.</b>
</i><br/><br/>Lexi and Austin both have secrets. She hides behind makeup and fake smiles, while he struggles to escape dangerous ties from his past.<br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410190201i/11072138.jpg' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Underneath her mask, Lexi is</span>
  <span id="freeText17464236991593724153" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410190201i/11072137._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="355" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book put me through the ringer. It was heartbreaking, painful and it left it's mark. I had to take a few breaks, <i>Sweet Fall</i> is not an easy read.<br><br><i>
  <b>We were both just too messed up to ever be with each other in the way we needed to be. Two shooting stars that burned out too quickly, never quite reaching each other's skies.</b>
</i><br><br>Lexi and Austin both have secrets. She hides behind makeup and fake smiles, while he struggles to escape dangerous ties from his past.<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410190201i/11072138.jpg" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Underneath her mask, Lexi is fragile and broken. One hateful comment has changed her. She has severe self image issues, and for the past few years she seems to have it somewhat under control. But when she decides to start cheering again, she finds herself falling down that dangerous path once again.<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410191788i/11072384._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="401" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Austin, the Crimson Tide's wide receiver, thought he had left his gang ties behind. With NFL hopes, he is doing everything he can to help his family. But with a sick mother and no money to pay for her care, he doesn't have much choice. His brother is selling drugs on campus and the dean has his sights set on Austin.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410194385i/11072679._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="435" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Bless their hearts. These two have all kinds of problems, their story is truly heartbreaking. <i>Sweet Fall</i> deals with some heavy issues, but I thought it was extremely well done. <br><br><i>
  <b>“It’s funny. I used to look up at the stars and feel so small and unimportant. But I’ve come to realize that the only thing that can ever make you feel alive and important is the one person who takes you for you.”</b>
</i><br></span>

<div id="review_1156000071" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1156000071" />
    <a title="Katy Loves Romance ❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10247668-katy-loves-romance"><img alt="Katy Loves Romance ❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1481665315p2/10247668.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1156000071?book_show_action=true">Jan 04, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katy Loves Romance ❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katy Loves Romance ❤️" href="/user/show/10247668-katy-loves-romance">Katy Loves Romance ❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10247668-katy-loves-romance?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10247668-katy-loves-romance?shelf=sports-men">sports-men</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10247668-katy-loves-romance?shelf=bad-boys">bad-boys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10247668-katy-loves-romance?shelf=top-favourite-reads-of-all-time">top-favourite-reads-of-all-time</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10247668-katy-loves-romance?shelf=2015-favourite-reads">2015-favourite-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10247668-katy-loves-romance?shelf=need-more-than-five-stars">need-more-than-five-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10247668-katy-loves-romance?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10247668-katy-loves-romance?shelf=6-star-reads">6-star-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10247668-katy-loves-romance?shelf=conquer-my-tbr-in-2015">conquer-my-tbr-in-2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1156000071" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11241354716180741193"><b>5***** VERY REAL STARS!!</b><br/><br/> <br/><a href='http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/886FFA0C-B682-4BB3-9E92-6253368ADE98_zpst0spvp1y.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421580042i/13388627._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 886FFA0C-B682-4BB3-9E92-6253368ADE98_zpst0spvp1y.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/> <br/> <br/>Ok Breathe I finished 1. this series the other night after being with these characters for over a week to two and 2. I finished Sweet Fall. This is not just a romance but more about LIFE, HEARTBRAKE and being DIFFERENT in this world and succeeding on being different. I'd say though to me the romance came second to the reason behind the story.<br/>I will also say this is so hard to review being that the subject matter was at times hard to read I had to put it down on occ</span>
  <span id="freeText11241354716180741193" style="display:none"><b>5***** VERY REAL STARS!!</b><br><br> <br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/886FFA0C-B682-4BB3-9E92-6253368ADE98_zpst0spvp1y.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421580042i/13388627._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 886FFA0C-B682-4BB3-9E92-6253368ADE98_zpst0spvp1y.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br> <br>Ok Breathe I finished 1. this series the other night after being with these characters for over a week to two and 2. I finished Sweet Fall. This is not just a romance but more about LIFE, HEARTBRAKE and being DIFFERENT in this world and succeeding on being different. I'd say though to me the romance came second to the reason behind the story.<br>I will also say this is so hard to review being that the subject matter was at times hard to read I had to put it down on occasions take a breather then go back in because this story really does come from the heart, this is Tillies book coming from her own experience so be aware this is no hearts and flowers read, yet I ADORED this more maybe although ROME in sweet home was one of the most gorgeous characters I've read this year so far Austin and Lexi's journey was BEAUTIFUL I find the hardest of journeys worth the time to read it makes us value our own lives and how thankful I am for not having that kind of pain on a daily basis.<br> <br>Ok I'm digressing... Let me explain!! <br><br><b>What's it about?</b><br>Austin aka Romes best friend comes from a dangerous background being part of a street gang which includes dealing class A Drugs, shooting being part of a pack as it were where brothers and family is all that matters but as he grew up he wanted a better life he didn't want to live like that not for himself, not for his 14 year old brother and not for his Momma, so he worked hard and found a way out working towards getting in the NFL, but there's also a fine line between his goal to become a professional football player and having the world and his loyalty to his family. Austin also has an older brother Axe who is very much in the dangerous world Austin has got out of and at any moment could bring him in if he needed him there therefore there's a battle between good and bad, what's right and wrong, what he wants to do and what he's TORN to do. <br> <br><br>Lexi has known of Austin because of Rome and Molly and that they are best friends to them but also because Lexi is a cheerleader and Austin is a college football player so they have known of each other for a while yet Lexi is in the wrong place at the wrong time and their first encounter is very unfortunate they are unable to spend time with each other because of circumstances that lexi was as and Austin ran into therefore they have to steer clear of each other yet they are drawn to each other due to the pain that they both see in each others demur. <br><br><br>Lexi has a disorder one where she controls everything that enters her mouth she's Anorexic and has inner thoughts inside her head that stops her from feeling and being happy, the core of the story I'd say would be around both Austin and Lexis journey. Although I loved the free flow and books 1 and 2 sweet fall was a much different journey where your sole focus is not <b>FOOTBALL </b>not <b>FRIENDSHIP</b> but <b>THEM.</b><br><br> <br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/BE57F931-69F1-46B6-8C8D-DCFA7AD2AF2C_zps7pp23r9x.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421580042i/13388628.jpg" alt=" photo BE57F931-69F1-46B6-8C8D-DCFA7AD2AF2C_zps7pp23r9x.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br> <br><br>Ok where do I start first off this story was about two people who had a façade against the people they were around their close friends didn't know what was going on, only them. <u>(appearances are deceiving right?)</u> and this is especially true in the case of Lexi she smiled over the top and portrayed the perfect cheerleader, the perfect friend and was always smiling to the people that needed to see those emotions in her yet underneath she was slowly loosing it, Austin saw who she truly was from get go as he too was doing the same thing. Austin is tough on the outside people were wary of who he was he was this fantastic footballer and had a bright future yet he had a very difficult home life and cause of that he was actually covering the scars he had on the inside. <br><br> <br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/2BFE9150-F024-41E8-8336-2B203C19CC9E_zpsyhljnmce.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421580042i/13388629._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 2BFE9150-F024-41E8-8336-2B203C19CC9E_zpsyhljnmce.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><i>So together they found something special they were unique and saw the scars that the other was hiding to the world.</i> <br><br> <br><b>
  <blockquote>"Do my scars repulse you?" ...... "No! Why would the scars repulse me? They're not who you are. they're from your past. They don't bother me at all. They don't bother me at all. It tells the story of your life." (.....) " <br><br><br>"just like your weight's no concern to me. You're you because you're you. I don't give a shit about weight or height. I look at true people. Real people. you're real, Pix. You got that shit in spades."</blockquote>
</b> <br><br> <br>This story is Raw and gritty and VERY REAL. It's about life and survival, I love stories like this because I FEEL something, I suppose its a close subject to me because I have three little girls and one 7 year old that doesn't like eating lots although is getting better but I constantly worry about her nutritional intake and as a mum I'm constantly finding different things to get her to eat properly what I'm saying is that as a girl to a teenager to a young adult and then as an adult as a woman there's so much competition to be perfect the perfect size, the perfect weight, the perfect look <b>PERFECTION</b> life's hard so this book was VERY REAL, you will feel emotional and sit and think and mull on life, expectations being happy sad to be <b>LOVED</b> I felt a whole lot throughout this journey. And I for one will be taking this lesson with me for a while. <br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/C5DE92D4-D9DD-4547-BEBC-4EE7504AECC5_zps59wy6hwa.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421580415i/13388661._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo C5DE92D4-D9DD-4547-BEBC-4EE7504AECC5_zps59wy6hwa.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The romance was secondary to me as I was so worried about their futures yet when they came together I was rooting for them to be together to get it on and find something in each other something that only they need, on the outside they looked weird but together they looked right, there is heartache and troubles for both Lexi and Austin. <br><br> <b>
  <blockquote>"She's my broken Pixie, and I'm her piece of Trailer trash scum."</blockquote>
</b> <br><br>I am loving Tillie's voice her writing is catchy I understood where she was I got pulled into her world straight away, honestly I haven't done much the past week due to not being able to walk away from these books so I need to catch up on life now, this was a story where I couldn't breathe and HAD to keep reading till I finished which is everything I enjoy in a book I cried I thought and I sat back and took breathers so yes it was HARD at times but it was also BEAUTIFUL. <br><br> <br>THANKYOU TILLIE &lt;3<br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/gifs/iloveyougif_zpsdb047c5a.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398803307ra/9466153.gif" alt=" photo iloveyougif_zpsdb047c5a.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br> <br><b>To Sum up</b><br>Will re-read this? ~ <b>Maybe in the future.</b><br>Will I read anything Tillie writes in the future? ~<b>Yes 100%</b><br>And will I recommend this book ~ <b>Yes absolutely.</b><br><br><a href="http://slutsistas.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417650623i/12469037._SX540_.png" height="90" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="11241354716180741193" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer16330243535282309283"><b>
  <u>***5 Beautiful Stars***!</u>
</b><br/><br/>This book was just superb. You know a book is good when days later the characters are <i>still</i> lingering with you! From the moment I opened this I was hooked. It usually takes time for me to warm up to the story, but from the very beginning I found myself completely invested and rooting for the characters. And now that I've read the last page and the book is done....the story still haunts me.<br/><br/>Austin is a footballer with dreams of making it to the NFL, but his awful family</span>
  <span id="freeText16330243535282309283" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>***5 Beautiful Stars***!</u>
</b><br /><br />This book was just superb. You know a book is good when days later the characters are <i>still</i> lingering with you! From the moment I opened this I was hooked. It usually takes time for me to warm up to the story, but from the very beginning I found myself completely invested and rooting for the characters. And now that I've read the last page and the book is done....the story still haunts me.<br /><br />Austin is a footballer with dreams of making it to the NFL, but his awful family life circumstances threatens to wreak havoc on everything he's working hard to achieve. Then there's the heroine Lexi, who struggles with her own inward battles. These two find each other in the most unlikely of ways...I absolutely LOVE unlikely romances and unusual characters that end up falling in love. <br /><br />I don't like to give too much of the story away, but this was an <b>epic love story</b>. <br />I cried <br />I empathized <br />I was angry<br />I was happy. <br />My emotions were pretty much all over the place. <br /><br />Would I recommend this book? A thousand times YES!!<br /></span>

<div id="review_1250830986" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1250830986" />
    <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts"><img alt="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1378340325p2/17755575.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1250830986?book_show_action=true">Apr 09, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts">Wendy&#39;sThoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Tillie Cole, Romance</span></div>

        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1250830986" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4992792663192911621"><b>5 Very Brave Stars<br/> * * * * * <i>Spoiler Free</i><br/>In 2013 Tillie Cole was introduced to me with her book, Sweet Home. My review expressed delight in the experience I had reading it. <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/752465741'>https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a> <br/>Her series continued and time being what it was, fleeting, I hadn't had the chance to catch up with all of her releases. Recently, she produced Sweet Hope to glowing reviews... but there was advisement of reading Sweet Fall first in order to appreciate Sweet Hope. Since I had a little </b></span>
  <span id="freeText4992792663192911621" style="display:none"><b>5 Very Brave Stars<br> * * * * * <i>Spoiler Free</i><br>In 2013 Tillie Cole was introduced to me with her book, Sweet Home. My review expressed delight in the experience I had reading it. <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/752465741">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a> <br>Her series continued and time being what it was, fleeting, I hadn't had the chance to catch up with all of her releases. Recently, she produced Sweet Hope to glowing reviews... but there was advisement of reading Sweet Fall first in order to appreciate Sweet Hope. Since I had a little time to tackle both books, I figured I would do what I told for once....<br><br>As I started Sweet Fall, not really having a clue about the storyline except the blurb and what I remembered from the first book, I read the intro from Tillie. Her letter to us was profound; it laid bare her life in ways most would never do...she decided to tackle a darkness she had experienced...a pain which riddled her days and nights...and she didn't hold back. She told us to take it as it happened from her experience... no one else's... not claiming her path was the happy ending we all crave... just something she must keep control of at all times.<br><br>It made me stop and ask myself if I was up to reading this... if I even wanted to read it knowing it wasn't the lighter fare I was in the mood for... The question was answered in a heartbeat because if she was brave and willing to share this with us...who was I to turn away.... and oh, I am so glad I did not.<br><br>All of us have demons... we all have things we fight within ourselves.</b> It starts with things when we were young...sometimes it is outside influences which cause us to doubt ourselves... or sometimes we are just managing the insecurities of young adolescences...something which isn't as life threatening as this story. Whatever the fear, doubt or question...each has weight in our development... and it is a crap shoot as to how one comment or action can trigger a lifetime of behavior due to the way it was processed. I truly think it is almost a chemical thing in how we are wired and how our lives up to that moment impact how we take all these things in...There is no judgement; it could be any one of us...and that is the importance of this tale.<br><br>We have two characters living lies with masks on at all times....one hiding the constant drain of being that happy girl cheerleader. Being friends and letting all think everything was a-ok when actually she was fighting 24/7 the pull to return and relinquish her life to the pursuit of perfect....perfect size, rib count....and weight. It has taken over her life before...isolating her and providing her with another doing the same battle, Daisey.... but she's left our girl ....and now Lexie is all alone with no one to confide in who understands this perfection and pull.<br><br>Our other character who is playing at being his own type of perfect as best he can; he is the wide receiver to Rome's Quarterback. He comes from a life where gangs are the parents and shields.... where his mother endured what no woman should have from her husband.... and then God laughed and gave her ALS. This was the motivator to hustling like his brother... the need for the medications for his sick mother...There was a once in a lifetime chance for him to make it out of that hell....a scholarship to play for the Tides. Even the older brother knew this was Austin's only chance... and he manipulated the gang to release him. <br><br>We have these two characters who have been circling each other through friends on the campus.... never really interacting but aware of who they are. A moment happens which brings them both crashing into each other at the worst time....Threats are made...additional fear is laid out for both with this new situation....Neither has any control of what could happen if the wrong elements get involved. They try to stay clear of each other....but fate wanted to lead these two to be together and they end up locked in a summerhouse overnight hiding from the dean and campus police. <br><br>It is during this time when things shift...comments are made... air is cleared and people recognizing the masks in place... like birds of the same species seeing they are the same in away....and it opens the mind and heart. For these two see through the pretend and talk to each other as real....not pushing too hard... for each has their pain and scars.<br><br>This story is so brave....it had me tearing during most of it. Austin's family and all of the drama surrounding it; the hopelessness of the situation and cruelty it imparted. There were times I was so frustrated by ego and stubbornness of the male characters not accepting financial assistance from their wealthy best friend. I got the need for men to be men and provide for their family but when it could be at the expense of others' healthcare... it is hard to accept. <br><br>Lexie's arc was heartbreaking. Women are constantly told how they should look and behave. Media tears down singers, actresses and even the First Lady of our country regarding size and weight. It is a wonder if a girl grows into a healthy adult today and not have a body issue.<br><br>The love Austin showed Lexie was pure and sweet. The mistakes in thoughts after their connection were unfortunate but understandable because of her history. The friends rallied for both Austin and Lexie when it was important and we got what was needed in the end. <br><br>The other characters were living and breathing off the page. We felt them all and the foundation for them came from the first book, Sweet Home. We knew of all of them and met more in depth Austin's brothers and mother. This family of strong Italians was tragic.... yet with beauty too. Each son brought something to the story and it is this family we are so interested in....<br><br>Tillie Cole placed a part of her soul on these pages sharing all the trauma and pain she personally has experienced with the hope of affecting at least one other person to get the assistance they may need...for them to see they are not alone in this world fighting this fight. Her writing affected me greatly and I am gratefully she wrote this book. I may not have suffered from the demons she did... but as I mentioned earlier... I don't think there is a person on this planet who hasn't felt not enough at one time or another...<br><br>I am now able to read Sweet Hope.... and am flying to the first page...you should, too. <br> <br><br> <br><strong>For more Reviews, Free E-books and Giveaways</strong><br><div>
  <br>
  <a href="http://starangelsreviews.blogspot.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img alt=" photo banner_zpsb3ab83a0.jpg" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407612151i/10746470._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</div></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer759937639" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11091883738927161565">4.5--<b>Pixie</b>--Stars!!!<br/><br/>Sweet Fall is a much heavier, darker, grittier read than Sweet Home. Both Lexi and Austin carry so much heartache and pain. Both putting on a facade. Hiding who they are from their friends. Pretending to be someone they aren't. <br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"Why the war paint, Pix?"<br/>"Because I can't stand the girl underneath..."<br/><br/>"Why the tattoos?"<br/>"Because I can't bear seeing the scars of my past."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408371962i/10841946._SX540_.jpg' height='250' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Lexi lives every day in fear. Of the demon that lurks in her head. The one that tells her she's not </span>
  <span id="freeText11091883738927161565" style="display:none">4.5--<b>Pixie</b>--Stars!!!<br><br>Sweet Fall is a much heavier, darker, grittier read than Sweet Home. Both Lexi and Austin carry so much heartache and pain. Both putting on a facade. Hiding who they are from their friends. Pretending to be someone they aren't. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"Why the war paint, Pix?"<br>"Because I can't stand the girl underneath..."<br><br>"Why the tattoos?"<br>"Because I can't bear seeing the scars of my past."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408371962i/10841946._SX540_.jpg" height="250" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lexi lives every day in fear. Of the demon that lurks in her head. The one that tells her she's not good enough. Not pretty enough. Not skinny enough. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"We all have secrets, Austin. Some people's are bigger than others, that's all."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Austin lives every day for someone else. A family he's trying to protect. Trying to free himself from the chains of his past. To save a brother from a life that will kill him. To help the mother that gave him everything. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"So you see, Pix, I have scars too. It's just mine are on the outside where everyone can see."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Two people brought together by fate. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408371237ra/10841883.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lexi tries to be stronger than the voice. To not let it bring her down. She hides from her friends. Her family. She denies the depth of her pain. She just wants to be normal. To not be ruled by what she sees and what she hears. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"All of this started with the rejection of a boy I liked....I want it to end with the acceptance of the boy I love."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Football is Austin's way out. His ticket to redemption. It's his only hope at a better life. For him and his family. A family tragedy brings Austin face to face with his past. A past that could take everything away. His future, Lexi, his friends, his family. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"We were both just too messed up to ever be with each other in the way we needed to be. Two shooting stars that burned out too quickly, never quite reaching each other's skies."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>For Austin, Lexi gives him something that is worth fighting for. To be the person she needs. And Austin gives Lexi hope. Hope that maybe Austin can silence the voice in her head. Hope that she can be beautiful for him. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1406321032i/10535485._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My heart broke for Lexi and Austin and what they both went through. It was so hard to read about the demons that took over Lexi. I wanted to punch <b>
  <i>him</i>
</b>, that voice in her head that ruled her life. Austin was the calm in Lexi's storm. He gave Lexi just a little bit of quiet. <br> <br>Austin's dedication and love for his family was inspiring. He was willing to give up everything to save his family, in the only way he knew how. He was proud, he was fierce, he was honorable. Lexi saw more than the bad-boy from the wrong side of the tracks. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"We all have secrets. Secrets well buried. Until we find the one soul who makes the burden of such secrets just a little bit easier to bear."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401176i/778335.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>ARC kindly provided by the author in exchange for an honest review</i>
</b> </span>
  <a data-text-id="11091883738927161565" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1476949083" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1476949083" />
    <a title="Sara➽ Ink Is My Sword" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword"><img alt="Sara➽ Ink Is My Sword" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603584262p2/28146945.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1476949083?book_show_action=true">Dec 23, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sara➽ Ink Is My Sword" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sara➽ Ink Is My Sword" href="/user/show/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword">Sara➽ Ink Is My Sword</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword?shelf=addictive">addictive</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword?shelf=best-book-dedications">best-book-dedications</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword?shelf=favorite-book-scenes">favorite-book-scenes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword?shelf=best-reviews">best-reviews</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword?shelf=character-driven-story">character-driven-story</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword?shelf=college">college</a>,

          </div>
