        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1476949083" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12868369855083063426"><b>5 “Dark Soul” Stars</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>“Why the war paint, Pix?<br/>Because I can't stand the girl underneath...<br/>"Why the tattoos ?"<br/>Because I can't bear seeing the scars of my past.”</i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><b>Is it normal that I wanna re-read it already??????????</b><br/><br/><b>Buddy-reading this with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/30036082-warda' rel='nofollow noopener'>the sweetest squishy ever!</a> Sharing this reading with someone made me love the book way more.</b><br/><br/>HOLY SHIT! I AM NOT KIDDING YOU THIS BOOKS GOT TO THE DEEPEST PARTS OF MY SOUL. IS PAINFUL, IS UGLY, IS TRIGGERING, IS RAW, IS BEAUTIFUL.<br/><br/><b>I WAS NOT READY FOR THE FEELS, A </b></span>
  <span id="freeText12868369855083063426" style="display:none"><b>5 “Dark Soul” Stars</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Why the war paint, Pix?<br>Because I can't stand the girl underneath...<br>"Why the tattoos ?"<br>Because I can't bear seeing the scars of my past.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>Is it normal that I wanna re-read it already??????????</b><br><br><b>Buddy-reading this with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/30036082-warda" rel="nofollow noopener">the sweetest squishy ever!</a> Sharing this reading with someone made me love the book way more.</b><br><br>HOLY SHIT! I AM NOT KIDDING YOU THIS BOOKS GOT TO THE DEEPEST PARTS OF MY SOUL. IS PAINFUL, IS UGLY, IS TRIGGERING, IS RAW, IS BEAUTIFUL.<br><br><b>I WAS NOT READY FOR THE FEELS, A SECURITY CAMERA CAUGHT ME IN THIS GIF:</b><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1514477658ra/24780979.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>WARNING:</b> Eating disorder, anxiety, emotions all over the freaking place. <br><br>When you start reading a novel and you are just at the dedication but you already feel your soul has been shaken, is because shit is gonna break you and you are gonna love this book. AKA ME. My friends, I was at chapter 6 and I was already tearing up, I don’t cry even in the most emotional books ever. This has to tell you something.<br><br><b>If you are looking for a fluffy, swooning, romantic, sexy NA book, sorry you are not gonna get that here. <br><br>THINGS I LOVED:<br><br>⇝DARKNESS/ UGLINESS </b><br><br>Tillie Colle touched upon ugly aspects of life, and she didn’t contain herself, she kept throwing arrows to tear me apart. She touches on anorexia, gang life, poverty, sickness, sorrow, anxiety, and insecurities. I loved how even in the sweetest scenes none of this fades because, in reality, it just doesn’t disappear. <br><br><b>⇝WRITING</b><br><br>It was beautiful, and I felt every single word deep in my bones. Even the curse words, because fuck yeah it added meaning and completed the characters personalities. The <i>voice</i> addition brought so much impact on the eating disorders storyline, is very much scary, because is like having an enemy 24/7 inside your head. I loved the parts where Tillie incorporated Italian. Fuck Austin talking Italian made me want to squish him <s> and maybe lick him honestly</s>. Also, the scenes with Austin’s mom were on point, I felt the struggle and devastation. <br><br><b>⇝CHARACTERS<br><br>Austin: </b>He is my ultimate crush on the bad boy, tortured soul, wanna protect you to death, type of character. He was in a gang, violence will always be part of his past but he honest to god is just a person who cares too much for everyone around him, trying to protect them even that means destroying himself. He was so tough but also a character full of sorrow and vulnerability. Every time he broke down, I broke down with him. I loved how even he was involved in all the deep shit, and stereotypical stuff, he wasn’t a playboy who slept with everyone crossing his path.<br><br><b>Lexi:</b> My god, this girl’s mind brought me to my knees with pain. I felt for her but also for all the people out there who have to undergo similar thought processing, I could relate. She really showed me that people could be wearing a huge armor and disguise and that what we get is not always true. <br><br>I felt like a mama bear trying to protect this two of all the shitty things life was throwing at them.<br><br><b>Axel:</b> FUCK YOU. I really don’t know how Tillie is gonna make me redeem him in the next book.<br><br><b>Levi:</b> Too precious, needs to be protected at all cost. A soul who lost his innocence too young.<br><br><b>⇝RELATIONSHIP</b><br><br>The romantic relationship is slow. Is almost like a hate-love, but it goes from fear-confidants-friendship-lovers. There is no immediate attraction or love at first sight, so thanks to the above for that. I loved how love didn’t alter the ugly reality the characters were living, it wasn’t the main thing. Also, the sex-scenes were on point. It wasn’t hot or smut but heartbreaking because of all the complications. I loved how Austin always asked if what he did was okay for our mc, it was sweet and caring. To be honest, I usually don’t root for to damaged characters to get together, but I completely wanted it in this story. I AM TRASH WHATEVER.<br><br><b>⇝MEANING</b><br><br>This book was close to the heart and experience of the author and I really appreciated it. The dedication and author's note had me expecting the whole story way more.<br><br><b>⇝CHAPTER 6 &amp; 10 My favs.</b> I will just say have tissues beside you because your heart will shatter. <br><br><br><b>THINGS I DIDN’T LIKE:<br><br>⇜ IT ENDED. </b>There were no more chapters to read and my heart broke because I need it, is air to me, necessary.<br><br><br><b>
  <i>“We were both just too messed up to ever be with each other in the way we needed to be. Two shooting stars that burned out too quickly, never quite reaching each other’s skies.” </i>
</b></span>

<div id="review_1025148589" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1025148589" />
    <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog"><img alt="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1518242765p2/14302918.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1025148589?book_show_action=true">Aug 12, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog">Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=buddy-reads">buddy-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=depressing">depressing</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1025148589" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7425536294843420865"><b>*****FOUR STARS*****</b><br/>(BR with Mel and Dee)<br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/cf2a41a26a05174f01966f2e64603a0b_zpsd351e69b.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411604773i/11254676._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo cf2a41a26a05174f01966f2e64603a0b_zpsd351e69b.jpg' width='335' height='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>So far, I have to say this series has been very enjoyable.<br/>I've now read four of Tillie Cole's books, and I can safely say the woman knows how to write a good story.<br/><br/><br/>This one was a bit on the sad side.<br/>Very depressing subject matter. One that hits close to home with me having had close friends that suffered from Anorexia and also since I am in a constant struggle myself over losing weight and staying in shape. I don't really know any woman who is 100% sa</span>
  <span id="freeText7425536294843420865" style="display:none"><b>*****FOUR STARS*****</b><br>(BR with Mel and Dee)<br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/cf2a41a26a05174f01966f2e64603a0b_zpsd351e69b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411604773i/11254676._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo cf2a41a26a05174f01966f2e64603a0b_zpsd351e69b.jpg" width="335" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>So far, I have to say this series has been very enjoyable.<br>I've now read four of Tillie Cole's books, and I can safely say the woman knows how to write a good story.<br><br><br>This one was a bit on the sad side.<br>Very depressing subject matter. One that hits close to home with me having had close friends that suffered from Anorexia and also since I am in a constant struggle myself over losing weight and staying in shape. I don't really know any woman who is 100% satisfied with how they look. Society places so much importance on looks and it's sad to say but I don't see that this will ever change.<br><br><br>We met Lexi Hart and Austin Carillo, in books 1 &amp; 2. Lexi is the goth cheerleader that is one of Molly's friends and sorority sisters. Austin is the wide receiver for the Crimson Tide and also best friend to Rome. These two have their own heartbreaking stories. <br><br><br><br>Lexi suffers from anorexia. She started when she was about 16 in High School and almost lost her life to the disease.<br>She's been in recovery for a few years. She had to be home schooled for quite a while and just recently was allowed to attend the university and join the Sorority and Cheer Squad.<br><br><br>I have to say I thought it was odd that her parents were hardly present in the story. They were portrayed as loving parents who really cared for her, so I am surprised they were hardly present in her life. You would think in reality, parents with a child who is suffering from this disease would be keeping a close eye on them. To make sure there weren't any signs of a relapse.<br>How her therapist wasn't taking her weight loss a little more seriously was also a little off for me. But I guess to build up the angst I can see why they may have been left out of the story.<br><br><br><br>Austin is the guy who grew up on the wrong side of the tracks. Living with his mom and two brothers in a trailer park.<br>His momma is a beautiful saint of a woman, who struggled through life, trying to provide for her three boys, after their father abandoned them all.<br>She is suffering from ALS, and without any healthcare benefits or money, the boys turn to a life of crime to come up with the money to pay for their mother's medication.<br><br><br>His older brother, Axel, joins a street gang, and gets Austin and his little brother Levi, sucked into the gang life as well. I really <b>HATED</b> Axel and I don't care what he did towards the end, in my book it's not enough to make amends. I am an older sibling, and I'd never let my little sister get involved in anything dangerous or illegal. Sorry, he's a character I didn't like and still don't care for. <br><br><br><br>One night while walking alone on campus, Lexi sees a drug exchange go down between Axel and a student. Axel is threatening her but Austin happens to show up at that moment and intervenes. Austin and Lexi get off on the wrong foot because of this situation. I had a hard time liking him in the beginning of the story because of how mean he was to Lexi. I couldn't see the appeal to Austin at all to be honest. The tattoos on his face just didn't make him sound attractive to me. I was thinking of Mike Tyson!! LOL<br>I don't approve of bullying and that's what he seemed to be doing to Lexi and I get he was trying to protect his family and his status at the University but to scare a timid and fragile looking girl, is just not ok with me.<br><br><br>Ultimately circumstances will eventually have these two falling for each other.<br>I was able to get on board with this and, <b>OH MY,</b> did I love every time Austin spoke in Italian to Lexi and his momma. My God that language just sounds so beautiful. I bet "honey take out the trash" even sounds romantic in Italian!! LOL <br><br><br>There were a couple of sexy time scenes but they weren't very steamy. Their first time was actually very heartbreaking.<br><br><br><i>
  <b>"And you have destroyed me, Pix, but never how I thought. You destroyed the fence I'd built up to keep people out. You destroyed the hard-ass persona I wore like a shield. But even more than that, you destroyed any reluctance I had to find comfort in someone else. You fuckin' bulldozed me, Pix. You, my tiny dark pixie, made all my defenses crumble to dust."</b>
</i><br><br><br><br>There's a bit of angst and Rome and the rest of the crew get involved. I was happy to get more of Rome!!<br>Lexi and Austin seemed to be two utterly broken souls whose love ended up being what saved them in the end.<br><br><br><b>I love you. I love you deeply, whole-heartedly, without hesitation, free of condition. I have fallen in love with you. The broken boy who has only ever known trouble and strife. Yet the broken boy who managed to put this broken girl back together, at least for a while.</b><br><br><br>I loved Austins' letter to Lexi and the ending. The epilogue was <b>BEAUTIFUL</b>!<br><br><br><i>
  <b>I know after today, I will never be alone with my fears. I know after today, my heart will be complete, joined eternally to the only man who has ever known how to love me in the way I needed to be loved.<br>He saved me. I saved him.</b>
</i><br><br><br>Well done, Tillie Cole!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="7425536294843420865" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer16463767281706349516"><b>4.5 "Why the war paint, Pix?" STARS</b><br/><br/>This was a heartbreakingly beautiful story! My emotions are all over the place.<br/><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/Gxq7fru' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422167066ra/13465585.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Knowing Ms. Cole, I expected <b>heart and soul</b> in this story and to be moved but I never expected the <b>depth of darkness and truth</b> that would be bared. Both main characters deal with some very real, harsh and life threatening issues.<br/><br/><b>Lexington "Lexi" Hart: "She sees...no beauty in...herself."<br/><a href='http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/Lexi_zps6a746670.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422166592i/13465527._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo Lexi_zps6a746670.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/><br/>Austin Carillo:"One broken boy carrying the weight of the world on his shoulders."</b><br/><a href='http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/Austin_zps31922c40.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>Each of </span>

</a><br><br>Knowing Ms. Cole, I expected <b>heart and soul</b> in this story and to be moved but I never expected the <b>depth of darkness and truth</b> that would be bared. Both main characters deal with some very real, harsh and life threatening issues.<br><br><b>Lexington "Lexi" Hart: "She sees...no beauty in...herself."<br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/Lexi_zps6a746670.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422166592i/13465527._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo Lexi_zps6a746670.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>Austin Carillo:"One broken boy carrying the weight of the world on his shoulders."</b><br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/Austin_zps31922c40.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><b>"That moment where you look at the same set of eyes you've gazed upon thousands of times before, only this time you see something more within their depths. This one time, it's as if you are looking down the lens of a spyglass and you can see into another's soul...and it seems to solder itself to yours."</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/rJkqxRV" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <span id="freeText14007225097663631449" style="display:none">4 "I'm beautiful... with you..." Stars!<br>(BR with Patty &amp; Dee)<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/738cb992-a436-45ec-8969-df64c62760c7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411408598i/11222875._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 738cb992-a436-45ec-8969-df64c62760c7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/9cfb63fc-ce70-48cd-b9bb-13d78a0b139a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411437935i/11228064._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 9cfb63fc-ce70-48cd-b9bb-13d78a0b139a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>-"What you see on the surface isn't always the reality."<br><br>-"We all have...secrets. Secrets well buried. Until we... find the one soul who... makes the burden... of such... secrets just that little bit... easier to... to... to bear."<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/Posters%20and%20quotes/61f63fea-7f1d-45b8-8ac0-52e2fe599703.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412004272i/11310354.png" alt=" photo 61f63fea-7f1d-45b8-8ac0-52e2fe599703.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Lexington Hart aka Lexi/Pix is a 21 yr. old senior attending the University of Alabama in Tuscaloosa, AL. She is a goth looking girl who is insecure &amp; is constantly fighting the pressure to be perfect. She battles dark thoughts &amp; her inner voice telling her she isn't good enough. Lexi keeps her secrets well hidden, and her friends don't truly know her. They aren't aware of her issues or poor self image. Everyone thinks she's a happy, normal college girl. <br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/457a03d5-c3d2-4f2a-919c-00a1152cacc1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411155084i/11198916.jpg" alt=" photo 457a03d5-c3d2-4f2a-919c-00a1152cacc1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>In an effort to gain back control of her life &amp; face her demons, Lexi joins the varsity cheer squad. She is a flyer for the Crimson Tide, &amp; this helps take her out of her comfort zone. She wanted a new life and to reinvent herself. After one of the games Lexi talks with one of the football players. His name is Austin Carillo aka Superstar. He's #83 for the Tide, &amp; one of the most promising wide receivers in the SEC. He's considered the Italian bad boy of UA.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/Posters%20and%20quotes/c01fa8e3-118c-4a12-b08a-70b80e705898.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412004134i/11310302.jpg" alt=" photo c01fa8e3-118c-4a12-b08a-70b80e705898.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>-"It's about fuckin' time, by the way!"<br><br>-"Are you talking to me?"<br><br>-Austin smirked in a deliciously dark way and gestured to my hair and face. "Yeah, I'm talking to you. It's about time a pompom chick 'round here broke the mold. It's good to have another one of us freaks on this team."<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/66a13b93-2d1c-41d2-ac60-7ef185003809.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412003893i/11310272.jpg" alt=" photo 66a13b93-2d1c-41d2-ac60-7ef185003809.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Austin is a gorgeous, ex-gang member from the wrong side of the tracks. His family is in a bad place, &amp; his potential NFL draft dreams is their only hope for a way out. He carries too much on his shoulders, &amp; is just trying to survive.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/f554767d-8ff7-4cf5-9a8d-ca47f2307e1a.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412003946i/11310280.png" alt=" photo f554767d-8ff7-4cf5-9a8d-ca47f2307e1a.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>-Austin was strong, he belonged to a dangerous gang, he had a dark past, but beneath his armor of tattoos, I sensed he also had a pure soul, and it was in distress.<br><br>-He was beautiful... and there was so much more to him than I ever imagined.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/6e4caac3-b846-4962-9271-aeb38a4ad8a9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411437132i/11227898.jpg" alt=" photo 6e4caac3-b846-4962-9271-aeb38a4ad8a9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>One evening Austin &amp; Lexi cross paths again under bad circumstances, &amp; become more tangled in each others lives. As they get to know each other they realize they are both under pressure, ashamed of who they are, &amp; hide behind a mask pretending to be something they aren't. He was like her, darker &amp; quieter, &amp; kept to himself.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/9d79c45b-c835-41d2-915d-0230f594c626.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411519973i/11243832._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 9d79c45b-c835-41d2-915d-0230f594c626.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>They end up growing closer, and finding comfort in each other. They finally have someone who they can share their secrets with &amp; they feel understands them. They are both broken, but help each other heal. They could just be themselves with each other. They trusted each other &amp; looked at one another &amp; saw more. Austin gave Lexi hope for the future, &amp; made her feel beautiful. Together they weren't so messed up, &amp; they saved each other with their love.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/Book%20ladies/Couples%20Pics/85d291d4-892f-417a-8b81-9ce526e9972c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412005320i/11310480.jpg" alt=" photo 85d291d4-892f-417a-8b81-9ce526e9972c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>-"I do want to know you more. Lord help me, but I do."<br><br>-Austin Carillo, the Italian boy from the wrong side of the tracks, kissed me. And it was magical. He made me feel safe and, for one glorious night, he made me feel beautiful.<br><br>-He was precious to me.<br><br>-Austin was the one person I could be my complete self with. There was no fakery, no acting around him; it was just me and him.<br><br>-Lexi looked up at me through long black lashes, and I felt as though my chest had ripped open and my heart was on display. It was that moment people talk about. That moment where you look at the same set of eyes you've gazed upon thousands of times before, only this time you see something more within their depths.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/b95a49d8-383b-4f1a-80e3-85770b869c27.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411520089i/11243851.jpg" alt=" photo b95a49d8-383b-4f1a-80e3-85770b869c27.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>-"You're safe in my arms, where you fuckin' belong."<br><br>-You are the most beautiful person I know, inside and out.<br><br>-I'd found a girl who got me heart and soul...<br><br>-She's everything to me.<br><br>-I knew in my heart what she meant to me... every-fuckin'-thing.<br><br>-I need you so much that I can't breathe.<br><br>-I'll always be there. <br><br>-BAMA VIDEO<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=w0Cb7bNibD0&amp;index=2&amp;list=RDo8Nj3WS-IsA">https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=w0Cb7...</a><br><br><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15162063715589973767">Do you ever read a book thats so beautiful, yet so tragic and painful when youre done you just don’t know what to do with yourself? Your heart is happy- but it still hurts so much. So you just sit and think about the book, cry some more and try to move on with a new read… that was my Sweet Fall experience. I did not expect this book to hit me so hard. I didn’t just cry a few tears, it was a river.<br/><br/>Then you finish the book way past your bedtime. Text your bestie and ask her ..,,,<br/><br/><b>WHY DO YOU HATE ME</b></span>
  <span id="freeText15162063715589973767" style="display:none">Do you ever read a book thats so beautiful, yet so tragic and painful when youre done you just don’t know what to do with yourself? Your heart is happy- but it still hurts so much. So you just sit and think about the book, cry some more and try to move on with a new read… that was my Sweet Fall experience. I did not expect this book to hit me so hard. I didn’t just cry a few tears, it was a river.<br /><br />Then you finish the book way past your bedtime. Text your bestie and ask her ..,,,<br /><br /><b>WHY DO YOU HATE ME?!!! Why do you have my tear ducts marked for death ?!!! Why would you let me read this book alone ?!!!!! Why why why why do you think I look good when I look sucker punched ??! </b> <br /><br />I can't breathe. Everything hurts. <br /><br /><br />Christy Baldwin, yes I plagiarized your review and yes I hate you, you torturous bestie bitch ❤️<br /><br />Paybacks. Remember. Paybacks.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9203885390884538136"><i> Words that come to mind after reading Sweet Fall...</i><br/><br/><i>
  <b>Beautiful...<br/> Heart Breaking...<br/> Meaningful...<br/> Intense...<br/> Tragic... <br/> Hope... </b>
</i><br/><br/>this book... this story.. insanely beautiful. It gripped my heart so hard and I sobbed.. but it also made me smile so big and feel so much joy. I loved it... Every. Single. Word. Tillie Cole is one of those writers that can grab hold of your heart with her words and squeeze it so tightly that you actually ache.. Such an amazing story. </span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1043260382" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7651600891880873170"><b>**** 4 Beautiful Broken Stars****</b><br/><br/><i>(BR with Mel and Patty)</i><br/><br/>This third book on the <i>Sweet Home</i> series was very emotional to say the least; Austin and Lexi have very complicated issues and both can relate with each other in always feeling lonely even though they are never alone…<br/><br/>Lexi is part of the cheer squad for the Crimson Tide and Austin is the star Wide Receiver of the team, they seen each other at games and around campus but one faithful night they will be forced together in a less than desirable</span>
  <span id="freeText7651600891880873170" style="display:none"><b>**** 4 Beautiful Broken Stars****</b><br /><br /><i>(BR with Mel and Patty)</i><br /><br />This third book on the <i>Sweet Home</i> series was very emotional to say the least; Austin and Lexi have very complicated issues and both can relate with each other in always feeling lonely even though they are never alone…<br /><br />Lexi is part of the cheer squad for the Crimson Tide and Austin is the star Wide Receiver of the team, they seen each other at games and around campus but one faithful night they will be forced together in a less than desirable situation. What starts with anger and fear soon turns into a relationship that will become their safe place, their escape from everything they are hurting from. Both Austin and Lexi feel like outcasts, even though they have a great group of friends who love them, they feel misunderstood and are constantly hiding behind walls but without knowing, the Pixy girl and the Bad Boy will come together and save each other in a <i>Sweet Fall.</i><br /><br /><i>
  <b>"Leaning forward, I kissed the tear away. And that's how we fell. Fell into sleep. Fell into trust. Fell for each other."</b>
</i><br /><br />When I first opened this book and read the authors note, I immediately knew this was going to be hard read, Tillie Cole bares her heart open to her readers with this story, which is in a way is her own story of struggle. Im sure this was no easy task and I commend her for being brave, for believing that from her pain someone can benefit or even be saved, if we all would use our pain to help others, we would live in a much better world, so <b>THANK YOU!!!!</b> Ms. Cole. <br /><br />This book was very different from Rome and Mol's story, it was heavier, darker but still beautiful. This is one very talented author, I've read a few of her books now and she always manages to ignite my senses and emotions, so I highly recommend any of her books to anybody who's not afraid to have their hearts squeezed in the name of a great love story… <br /><br />This book was full of amazing music and there is a playlist at the end of the book, and this were my favorite songs:<br /><br />*Beautiful With You by Halestorm<br />*All I Need by Within Temptation <br />*Shake it Out by Florence and The Machine<br />*Sky Full Of Stars By Coldplay<br />*That I would Be Good by Alanis Morissette.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7651600891880873170" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_762027086" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/762027086" />
    <a title="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog"><img alt="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1416791332p2/4597644.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/762027086?book_show_action=true">Nov 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" href="/user/show/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog">Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=i-want-it-now">i-want-it-now</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=lead-character-tattooed-and-sexy">lead-character-tattooed-and-sexy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=dual-pov">dual-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=hot-and-heavy">hot-and-heavy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=must-re-read-again">must-re-read-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=crack-books">crack-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=new-adult-mature-ya">new-adult-mature-ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=highly-emotional">highly-emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=lead-character-bad-boy">lead-character-bad-boy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=lead-character-s-sports-star">lead-character-s-sports-star</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer762027086" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9075719577874507239">Five Heartbreaking & Soul-crushing Stars<br/><br/><a href='http://s1094.photobucket.com/user/thessamari/media/SweetFallMeme1_zps34957553.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405401650i/10392577._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo SweetFallMeme1_zps34957553.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>
  <i> “Why the war paint, Pix?”<br/>“Because I can’t stand the girl underneath,” she whispered<br/><br/>“Why the tattoos?” Lexi asked<br/>“Because I can’t bear seeing the scars of my past.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>Even before I begin writing this review, I already know expressing my feelings in words is going to be difficult. <br/>This story, my God, this story…<br/>I’m going to be straight up honest with you guys. This was not an easy read. This was emotional, raw and truly heartbreaking. Yes, this is a lo</span>
  <span id="freeText9075719577874507239" style="display:none">Five Heartbreaking &amp; Soul-crushing Stars<br><br><a href="http://s1094.photobucket.com/user/thessamari/media/SweetFallMeme1_zps34957553.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405401650i/10392577._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo SweetFallMeme1_zps34957553.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i> “Why the war paint, Pix?”<br>“Because I can’t stand the girl underneath,” she whispered<br><br>“Why the tattoos?” Lexi asked<br>“Because I can’t bear seeing the scars of my past.”</i>
</b><br><br>Even before I begin writing this review, I already know expressing my feelings in words is going to be difficult. <br>This story, my God, this story…<br>I’m going to be straight up honest with you guys. This was not an easy read. This was emotional, raw and truly heartbreaking. Yes, this is a love story, but it was so much more than boy meets girl and fall in love. Oh no…it was so much more than that. <br><br><b>
  <i>“I don’t look up at the stars to feel inferior, Austin. All I have to do is open my eyes and look at myself in the mirror.”</i>
</b><br><br>Lexi is hiding a dangerous secret behind her cheerful smile and Goth makeup. She’s fought so hard to be where she is today - back in college, and even cheering for the Tide. But everyday she fights to keep her secret - to keep the <i>voice</i> at bay. She will never be fully <i>cured</i>. Her triggers are always present and it doesn’t take much for her to fall, especially when a boy from the wrong side of the tracks enters her life. <br><br><b>
  <i>All anyone ever saw when they looked at me was the white trash ex-gang member from the Heighterfamed trailer park across town.<br>But not her.<br>Fuck knows why, but Pix only ever saw more.</i>
</b><br><br>Austin Carillo is so close to achieving his dream of making the NFL and finally being able to help his family get out of their tragic situation. He’s known as the star wide receiver for the Tide with a dangerous past. So far Austin has been able to stay clear of his drug-dealing-ex-gang past, but things are starting to spiral out of control again. His mother is extremely sick and his brothers are desperate to amend the situation, even to go as far as dealing in his own campus. His decent back is jeopardizing everything he’s fought for, especially when the one person that can bring it all down is the same person who can also be his salvation. <br><br><b>
  <i>I will cherish the sweetest, most beautiful fall…With Austin Carillo, my home.</i>
</b><br><br>This story opened up my mind and thoroughly shredded my heart. Austin and Lexi’s story is one that I won’t be forgetting. This is a dual POV and being inside their respective heads was certainly painful at times. The constant struggles to just keep their head above water, and their need to fight their demons was tough to intake. As I said before, this was not an easy read. This had a darker vibe than the first two books but that’s only because Austin and Lexi are a bit darker than the other characters in the series. With that said, this can actually be read as a standalone, though there are spoilers from the first two books. <br><br>Thank you, Tillie, for sharing this story. The topics addressed are rooted deep and the strength it took to write it shines through the pages. Bravo!<br><br>-----<br><b>
  <u>♥♥♥ FOLLOW ME ♥♥♥</u>
</b><br><a href="http://s1094.photobucket.com/user/thessamari/media/Banner2_zps7a6c719e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379801013i/678281.jpg" alt=" photo Banner2_zps7a6c719e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_1010779494" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1010779494" />
    <a title="Christie«SHBBblogger»" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6650940-christie-shbbblogger"><img alt="Christie«SHBBblogger»" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1537729030p2/6650940.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1010779494?book_show_action=true">Jul 29, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christie«SHBBblogger»" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christie«SHBBblogger»" href="/user/show/6650940-christie-shbbblogger">Christie«SHBBblogger»</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=na">na</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=broken-heroine">broken-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=advanced-copy">advanced-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=has-a-playlist">has-a-playlist</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=august2014">august2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1010779494" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15996155577208926017"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1489274209i/22201529.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Title:</b>Sweet Fall <br/><b>Series:</b>Sweet Home #3<br/><b>Author:</b>Tillie Cole<br/><b>Release date: </b>August 26, 2014<br/><b>Rating:</b>4 stars<br/><b>Cliffhanger:</b>No<br/><b> HEA: </b> <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[Yes  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1489274209i/22201528.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408457794i/10853455._SY540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Sweet Fall is darker than what I was expecting. Sweet Home was...sweet. It was a feel good book about a romantic College romance with a star athlete and an intellectual girl who didn't really fit in. So it came as a surprise how different this book turned out to be. This book is about the outcasts. One because of where he was born, the other be</span>
  <span id="freeText15996155577208926017" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1489274209i/22201529.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Title:</b>Sweet Fall <br><b>Series:</b>Sweet Home #3<br><b>Author:</b>Tillie Cole<br><b>Release date: </b>August 26, 2014<br><b>Rating:</b>4 stars<br><b>Cliffhanger:</b>No<br><b> HEA: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1489274209i/22201528.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408457794i/10853455._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sweet Fall is darker than what I was expecting. Sweet Home was...sweet. It was a feel good book about a romantic College romance with a star athlete and an intellectual girl who didn't really fit in. So it came as a surprise how different this book turned out to be. This book is about the outcasts. One because of where he was born, the other because of a disease that eats away at her mind. This isn't a fluff filled New Adult story filled with hooking up, flirting, and meaningless conflicts. This book is raw, real, and contains serious life issues. It isn't always pretty, and it's characters don't always do what society deems right. Sometimes choices are taken from you. Sometimes life takes you places you never want to visit again. Sometimes you fall.<br><br>Lexi puts on a dark mask. In every sense of the word.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408458631i/10853546._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She uses it to cover up all the hurt, everything she wants to hide from the world. She's just been deemed "recovered" from Anorexia. A disease that ripped her life apart and changed her forever. She escaped with her life despite the voice nagging her in her mind that she's not enough. That voice that continues to taunt her no matter how much she tries to ignore it. That same voice that took her best friend away, and she's not sure she can avoid the same fate.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408460340i/10853697.jpg" width="500" height="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> She's not your typical cheerleader...she has the whole goth painted face and wears all black. She seems scary on the outside, but on the inside, she's very breakable and very alone.<br><br><b>She seemed so small. Seemed so fragile. Like the littlest thing could destroy her.</b><br><br>Austin was a hardcore, edgy guy who's whole life has only experienced hardship and scorn. His mother is the only positive thing in his life and she's slipping away from him through a disease that he and his brothers can't afford to fight. He grew up in poverty, falling into gang life, but managed to escape through his talent in football. But the taint never went away. He'll always be the guy who can't be trusted. To stay far away from. Lexi and Austin get tangled up in the worst possible way-she's a witness to his brother's crime on campus and she's the one person who could crush his entire future. <br><br><u>They begin with fear, hate, and intimidation. </u><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408459910i/10853647.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>He hated me, and I feared him. But I did care. I cared so deeply that he'd seen the real me. The girl who didn't measure up. The girl with too many flaws.</b><br><br>But neither can deny that they see likeness in each other's eyes. They see understanding. But most of all, they see acceptance. Something that they both need like air to breathe.<br><br><b>Ain't no one ever looked upon me with such grace, with such trust before, and I felt humbled that she chose to gift it to me.</b><br><br>They have to meet in secret. Being publicly together could end in disaster. Dangerous. So they are each other's secret place of comfort. They can unload their burdens on each other and for the first time, feel free to be their true selves. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408972310i/10916402._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When Austin tries to push Lexi away and protect her from the choices that he's being forced to make, they both lose their grip and their security. This book was difficult to read in parts because of what this couple has to live through. Lexi is overcome with doubts, crippling insecurities, and her small shoulders are heavy with the weight of it all. Austin is living through the hell of seeing his mother suffer and the having to choose between his entire future or doing things, things he never wanted to be a part of again and ease her pain. The last section of the book is tense and difficult-I was really hurting for these two broken souls.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408461265i/10853781._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The one thing that bothered me was the scene where Lexi's father accepts Austin based on reading Lexi's diary and seeing how deeply she feels about him. I'm sorry, I didn't see that ever happening. He accepts him solely based on the fact that he made her happy? Even though he's covered in tats and piercings from head to toe, has dealings with a gang, and the absolute worse reputation? <i>And</i> he knows exactly <i>what</i> he's been doing in that gang? As a parent, I can tell you, it wouldn't be that easy to accept him for my daughter, no matter what the circumstances. <br><br>This book was much more than I was expecting to get. It was bravely written by the author about a topic that is very much a part of her and that honesty can be seen shining through the story. This disease is a true battle every day and I can't imagine living and struggling with it. If you want to read a book that will hit your heart and make you feel, look no further. It's a great story of healing and redemption and acceptance. It's not an easy love story but a story that's gritty and genuine. Another great read by Tillie Cole.<br><br><i>**ARC provided for blog tour in exchange for an honest review**</i><br><br><b>FOLLOW SMOKIN HOT BOOK BLOG ON: <b><br><br><a href="https://twitter.com/BlogSmokin/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img alt="Twitter" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391768351i/8452934.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="http://facebook.com/smokinhotbookblog" target="_blank"     <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1522753434" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1522753434" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1522753434?book_show_action=true">Jan 23, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=pb-i-own">pb-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=feeeeels">feeeeels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series-standalone">series-standalone</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1522753434" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9365420083002118829"><b>4.5 heart-shattering stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454338719ra/17947699.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>After reading (and LOVING) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18105011.Sweet_Home__Sweet_Home___1_' title='Sweet Home (Sweet Home, #1) by Tillie Cole' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sweet Home</a>, I was really excited to continue on with this series and thought I knew exactly what to expect. Oh, how wrong I was. Tillie Cole stunned me with the depth and emotional intensity of this book. She made me fall in love with two broken souls, both struggling with the demons of their past and desperately trying to find some happiness, and then she broke my heart, ripped it from my body and stomped all over it before putting it all bac</span>
  <span id="freeText9365420083002118829" style="display:none"><b>4.5 heart-shattering stars</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454338719ra/17947699.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>After reading (and LOVING) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18105011.Sweet_Home__Sweet_Home___1_" title="Sweet Home (Sweet Home, #1) by Tillie Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Sweet Home</a>, I was really excited to continue on with this series and thought I knew exactly what to expect. Oh, how wrong I was. Tillie Cole stunned me with the depth and emotional intensity of this book. She made me fall in love with two broken souls, both struggling with the demons of their past and desperately trying to find some happiness, and then she broke my heart, ripped it from my body and stomped all over it before putting it all back together again. She has given us a beautiful, insightful story with a heartachingly gorgeous romance that held me absolutely captivated - I read it in one sitting, unable to put it down – and I absolutely loved it.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“We all have secrets … Some people’s are bigger than others, that’s all.”</i>
</blockquote><br>Lexi and Austin were both introduced in Sweet Home. Lexi is the quiet but perky goth girl who is friends with Molly, and Austin is the tattooed and pierced football-playing best friend of Rome. The timeline of this story matches up with events in <i>Sweet Home</i>, so Molly and Rome’s storyline is playing out in the background of everything that is happening with Lexi and Austin, so I’d recommend starting with that one first. But if you think from that book you can guess Lexi and Austin’s history, or predict how their story will play out, guess again.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>Sometimes, someone could stumble unannounced into the train wreck that is your life and begin to pull you out of the heavy rubble weighing down on your chest.</i>
</blockquote><br>Lexi’s cheery personality is a façade that she puts on to hide her deadly secret <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ she suffers from severe anorexia <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. She hides behind goth make-up and shapeless clothes, putting on a cheerful front so that nobody knows the horror that she lives with, and nobody sees the real her – the girl that she loathes. After years of therapy, she has put herself out there for the first time since she was 16 and has fulfilled her dream of attending college and being a cheerleader. And though she is technically ‘cured’, her demons continue to plague her. Her recovery is a day-by-day effort, and every day is a mental struggle that she must fight to remain healthy. And bravo to Tillie Cole for writing Lexi the way that she did, and for putting so much heart into this brave but terrified girl and her often misunderstood illness. Her battle is realistically and hauntingly written, and gives a chilling insight into people struggling with the disorder. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“I don’t need to look up at the stars to feel inferior, Austin. All I have to do is open my eyes and look at myself in the mirror.</i>
</blockquote><br>Austin’s home life was always difficult. He is the middle of three brothers, and was raised by a wonderfully loving mother after their father left; but they were dirt poor, living in a trailer in a bad neighbourhood and when their mother became ill, Austin’s older brother, Axel was drawn into a notorious and violent gang, dealing drugs and doing whatever else was necessary in order to make money to keep a roof over their heads and pay for their Mamma’s treatments. Soon Austin was sucked into the life, but was able to escape to attend college and play football on a scholarship - a future in the NFL would secure his family’s future. But now, with him close to graduation and his mother only getting sicker, Austin’s younger brother Levi is being pulled into the gang, and Austin himself is never far enough away from the lifestyle and the danger that surrounds it, and suddenly all that he has worked for is under threat. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“You see, Pix, I have scars too. It’s just mine are on the outside where everyone can see.</i>
</blockquote><br>Lexi and Austin are thrust into each other’s lives in the worst of circumstances. Lexi sees something she shouldn’t, immediately becoming the one person who can destroy Austin’s family, and in order to protect them, he has to be the big badass who threatens her to keep quiet. It’s an awful beginning for them, and when their friends hook up, it leads to lots of awkward encounters, but things slowly start to shift. Lexi and Austin recognise something in each other – a hidden pain that is sadly familiar – and as their private lives unexpectedly begin to intersect more often, they start to open up to each other. And in each other they find comfort, understanding and acceptance that neither of them realised they needed, somebody to talk to and take comfort from. And as they grow closer, feelings start to develop, and I fell right along with them.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Pix, I need you”…<br>“I think…I think I might need you too.”</i>
</blockquote><br>Their relationship develops naturally and realistically, and I loved every moment of it! And it’s not all emo and broody, they have fun together too and they cherish those lighter, happy moments. Austin’s circumstances mean that their relationship has to be kept quiet in order to keep Lexi safe, and that added a really nice sense of ‘specialness’ as they exist in their little bubble, being each other’s touchstone and support in the mayhem of their lives. They are both hiding terrible and painful secrets, yet they are so open with each other, and I love that they were able to find something so important, unexpected and special, despite all that they were dealing with. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“You fuckin’ bulldozed me, Pix. You, my tiny dark pixie, made all my defences crumble to dust.”</i>
</blockquote><br>But privately, things are deteriorating, and fighting off their demons becomes near impossible. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>I’m lost without you.<br>I can’t breathe without you.<br>Without you here, all I can do is fall…</i>
</blockquote><br>OMG, the feels! You know what’s coming, and you know it’s going to be bad, but when it happened, it just gutted me! I was in tears for the last few chapters of the book, devastated by everything that happened and the emotion that Cole managed to pour into it all. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>When you’re ready, look up. I am waiting for you, baby. I’ll always be there, waiting for you.</i>
</blockquote><br>Waaaaaaaaail!!!!!<br><br>Part of Lexi and Austin’s struggles with their pasts is hiding who they really are, sometimes not even acknowledging it to themselves, and I thought the slow reveal of everything that they are, and everything that they feel was really well written, and a wonderful way to reflect their deepening relationship. This book is as much a story of Lexi and Austin’s personal journeys as it is a story of them together, and I thought the balance of personal growth and the healing that comes from finding love, true acceptance, and somebody to depend on, was really well done<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“We all have secrets. Secrets well buried. Until we find the one soul who makes the burden of such secrets just that little bit easier to bear.”</i>
</blockquote><br>This is a beautifully written story. Full of drama, angst, torment and heartache, it’s also incredibly uplifting, with an amazing love story, and an epilogue that finishes everything off beautifully.<br><br>I loved it – 4.5 stars<br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="9365420083002118829" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_841148155" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/841148155" />
    <a title="✦❋Arianna✦❋" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23370948-arianna"><img alt="✦❋Arianna✦❋" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420671997p2/23370948.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/841148155?book_show_action=true">Feb 01, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✦❋Arianna✦❋" class="user" itemprop="url" name="✦❋Arianna✦❋" href="/user/show/23370948-arianna">✦❋Arianna✦❋</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer841148155" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6992988881811382620"><b>4.5 STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409139300i/10938491.jpg' width='400' height='420' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"We all have secrets, Austin. Some people’s are bigger than others, that's all."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1409139448ra/10938509.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>Sweet Fall</i> is the third book in Tillie Cole’s <i>Sweet Home</i> series. Full of angst, gritty and raw, this it’s not your typical romance. Very different from <i>Sweet Home</i>, the first book in the series, <i>Sweet Fall</i> tells the story of two people who try to fight their own demons. Together they will fight, they will love, they will fall. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1409139573ra/10938540.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Lexington Hart (Lexi) is faking everything in her life. She is scared,</span>
  <span id="freeText6992988881811382620" style="display:none"><b>4.5 STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409139300i/10938491.jpg" width="400" height="420" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"We all have secrets, Austin. Some people’s are bigger than others, that's all."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1409139448ra/10938509.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Sweet Fall</i> is the third book in Tillie Cole’s <i>Sweet Home</i> series. Full of angst, gritty and raw, this it’s not your typical romance. Very different from <i>Sweet Home</i>, the first book in the series, <i>Sweet Fall</i> tells the story of two people who try to fight their own demons. Together they will fight, they will love, they will fall. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1409139573ra/10938540.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Lexington Hart (Lexi) is faking everything in her life. She is scared, she is broken and she lives every day in fear. Insecurities haunt her each and every day and she doesn’t know if she’s strong enough to stop the voices. The voices are controlling, negative and they never stop. She’s never skinny enough and she’s never good enough. Lexi is trying to fight this agonizing disorder,anorexia, but she fears every day. She fears the voices will get what they want. Hinding behind her makeup and her goth look, Lexi is playing just a role.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"So you see, Pix, I have scars too. It's just mine are on the outside where everyone can see."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1409139897ra/10938594.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Austin Carillo is a wide receiver for the Crimson Tide. He wants to make it to NFL, to have a future, to help his family, but with his past nothing it's for sure. Living in a trailer all his life in an ill-famed neighborhood, Austin's family is poor. He manage to stay away from The Heighters, his ex-gang for two years. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>All anyone ever saw when they looked at me was the white trash ex-gang member from the Heighter-famed trailer park across town.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>With his mother, who is very sick and with a constant pressure from his ex-gang his future is uncertain, he doesn’t know where he will be - with The Heighters or in the NFL.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409139897i/10938595.png" width="400" height="550" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lexi and Austin meet under unfortunate circumstances. They are drown to each other from the beginning and soon after they became friends. Austin is the only one who figures out that Lexi’s makeup is her shield, because his tattoos are his. They form a bond and even if they are so different, they are similar too. They trust each other and they confide their past and fears. They found solace in one another and in the end they save each other.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“We all have secrets. Secrets well buried. Until we find the one soul who makes the burden of such secrets just that little bit easier to bear.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><i>Sweet Fall</i> was a beautiful, emotional, gut wrenching story. The realness of this story is so heartbreaking and like me you will be emotionally overwhelmed after reading this. Reading this you will <b>FEEL</b>.<br><br>The premise of this story was new to me. Even if I knew that it will be an emotional read, I never expected to be so moved by this story and by these characters. My heart broke so many times reading this. It broke for Lexi and Austin, it broke for Levi, it broke for Austin’s mother. <br><br>The characters are so unique and so well developed in this story. I loved both Lexi and Austin. Austin is a great hero. Loyal to his family, tender with his mother, supportive, caring and patient with Lexi, he melted my heart. I loved him for the fact that he sees Lexi how she really is, beautiful and that he respects her boundaries. Lexi is such a strong woman. She is a fighter and I admired for that. She has such a big heart. To read her story was difficult and frustrating at times, maybe because I was never anorexic, but there were so many times when I wanted to give her a hug. <br><br>Overall, this book was amazing. Beautifully written, <i>Sweet Fall</i> will definitely touch your heart! I highly recommend reading this book!<br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="6992988881811382620" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1024323447" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1024323447" />
    <a title="~♡AB♡~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12180287-ab"><img alt="~♡AB♡~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1555104554p2/12180287.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

She's pretty emo and she constantly fights a voice in her head telling her she needs to reach perfection by not eating, that she needs to be thinner.<br/><br/><b>Austin Carillo</b> is the heavily tattooed wide receiver on the college football team.   <span id="freeText7449402847301179344" style="display:none">4.5 <b>un piccolo folleto</b> Stars.<br><br>Meet Austin and Lexi. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409217591i/10949846._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Lexi Hart</b> is a cheerleader for the Tide football team, she has returned to the squad after 4 years. She has a secret which she hides beneath her baggy clothes and heavy make up. She's pretty emo and she constantly fights a voice in her head telling her she needs to reach perfection by not eating, that she needs to be thinner.<br><br><b>Austin Carillo</b> is the heavily tattooed wide receiver on the college football team. Born to Italian parents, he has a strong connection to his Mamma, and his 2 brothers, but when he finds out that his former gang the "Heighters" have recruited his baby brother, he realises he would do anything to protect his family. <br><br>When Lexi oversees Austin's brother doing a drug deal on campus, Austin scares the crap out of her, threatening bad things if she tells a soul. If he gets kicked off the team because of his brother, he won't be able to step up and get his family the hell out of there.<br><br>After discovering his Mamma is dying, Lexi turns out to be the only person he can talk to. He gets close to no-one, but he is drawn to Lexi like a moth to a flame and she sees something in him that helps the voice keep quiet. They share a love of the stars, and meet in secret to share their secrets.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409220258i/10950131._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Their story was heartbreaking, I got really emotional and I applaud the author for writing something that was so personal to her. <div id="review_1449282613" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1449282613" />
    <a title="Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog"><img alt="Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420222674p2/38657470.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1449282613?book_show_action=true">Nov 22, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)" href="/user/show/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog">Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/22919478-sweet-fall">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=not-just-a-keg-party">not-just-a-keg-party</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=4-stars">4-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=jock-straps-r-us">jock-straps-r-us</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1449282613" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15546004980794988099">Don’t let the fact that <i>Sweet Fall</i> is a sports romance set on a college campus deceive you. This isn’t a New Adult romantic comedy – at all. It deals with some heavy subject matter, but it still manages to be… well… sweet.<br/><br/>Lexi and Austin are two college seniors who are each living inauthentic lives. To their friends, Lexi is the perky emo cheerleader, and Austin is the strong NFL-bound football player. In reality, they both wear masks to protect their insecurities, fears, and dark secrets. Their</span>
  <span id="freeText15546004980794988099" style="display:none">Don’t let the fact that <i>Sweet Fall</i> is a sports romance set on a college campus deceive you. This isn’t a New Adult romantic comedy – at all. It deals with some heavy subject matter, but it still manages to be… well… sweet.<br><br>Lexi and Austin are two college seniors who are each living inauthentic lives. To their friends, Lexi is the perky emo cheerleader, and Austin is the strong NFL-bound football player. In reality, they both wear masks to protect their insecurities, fears, and dark secrets. Their friendship gets off to a rocky start when they meet, but soon they recognize a kindred spirit with concealed pain. Safe from judgments, they begin to let their masks slip around each other.<br><br>The book is well written and quite thought provoking. Outward appearances can be so deceiving. How well do we really know what goes on inside someone’s life? I won’t delve into the secrets both characters are hiding, but <i>Sweet Fall</i> is very eye opening in its frank examination of stigmatized social issues. While the romance between Lexi and Austin is featured heavily, it’s the social issues and the importance of family that are the focal points of the story.<br><br><i>Sweet Fall</i> is a continuation of the Sweet Home series and although it can be read as a standalone, it is more meaningful if you read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18105011.Sweet_Home__Sweet_Home___1_" title="Sweet Home (Sweet Home, #1) by Tillie Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Sweet Home</a> first.<br><br><a href="http://readingfrenzyblog.com" target="”_blank”" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445822108i/16706599.jpg" alt="Reading Frenzy Book Blog" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="15546004980794988099" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1028951577" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2404697906953860103"><b>“It’s funny. I used to look up at the stars and feel so small and unimportant. But I’ve come to realize that the only thing that can ever make you feel alive and important is the one person who takes you for you."</b><br/><br/>What an amazing quote to really drive home the meaning behind Lexington Hart and Austin Carillo's story. Two characters from opposite worlds with tragic backgrounds defining them. They wear facades for all to see while secretly knowing their personal truths. From everyone in their lives</span>
  <span id="freeText2404697906953860103" style="display:none"><b>“It’s funny. I used to look up at the stars and feel so small and unimportant. But I’ve come to realize that the only thing that can ever make you feel alive and important is the one person who takes you for you."</b><br><br>What an amazing quote to really drive home the meaning behind Lexington Hart and Austin Carillo's story. Two characters from opposite worlds with tragic backgrounds defining them. They wear facades for all to see while secretly knowing their personal truths. From everyone in their lives...they hide...<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409518803i/10988404.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><b>"Why the tattoo's Austin?"</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409518803i/10988405._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>A single question posed to a roughneck "Heighter's for life" man. A football superstar trying to make a life for his famiglia. He is hard and strong, yet vulnerable and so good hearted. He is different from the norm around 'Bama football, a freak perhaps.<br><br><b>"Why the war paint Pix?"</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409518803i/10988406.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>A petite girl with a good heart and terrible self image. She lives everyday in constant battle with a voice inside her head telling her she is not good enough. Conscious of every aspect of her body, she is slowly losing her fight to "live" healthy.<br><br>What an unlikey pairing of couples...what a perfectly imperfect love story of epic proportions!<br><br>In a strong emotional tale, Lexi and Austin find that when true love exists, the façade slips and only the inner beauty is seen. There is a push to be better, to do better...a true NEED for one another.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409518803i/10988407.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>In the face of violence, fear, and even death...there is true beauty in strength. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409518803i/10988408.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For me this book is profound! It is going right up to the top of my 2014 favorite list! Tillie Cole wrote Lexi's struggle with such honesty and raw emotion that I found myself wiping away tears as I read her innermost thoughts. As for Austin...I find myself a bit speechless when it comes to his character. His loyalty to his friends and family is unmatched, his love and sacrifice for his mother is moving, and the fight for his Pix is amazing. <br><br>Thank you Tillie Cole for this truth...If one person struggling to accept their image can grasp onto the hope this inspires then you have surpassed so much more than writing a successful book!</span>
